INSERT INTO peptides
SELECT DISTINCT b.bioentry_id, pep.peptide, pep.f061400, pep.f061401, pep.f061402,
		pep.f061403, pep.f061404, pep.f061405, pep.f061406, pep.f061407
FROM unsorted_peptides pep, biosequence bioseq
INNER JOIN bioentry b 
ON INSTR(b.description, pep.protein) AND INSTR(bioseq.seq, pep.peptide)
